# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 06:30:21.748007

### Base Program

```py
def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def maxTasks(tasks, workers, pills, strength):
  tasks.sort()
  workers.sort()

  cnt = 0
  i = 0
  for j in range(pills):
    while i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] > workers[j] + strength:
      i += 1
    if i < len(tasks):
      cnt += 1
      i += 1

  i = 0
  for j in range(pills, len(workers)):
    if i < len(tasks) and tasks[i] <= workers[j]:
      cnt += 1
      i += 1
      
  return cnt



```
